rating:4.7
posted:Posted June 9, 2023
msg:I have stayed here several times when visiting Shanghai and I have always had a pleasant experience.   The room is clean with a sort of stylish minimalism, but it has everything that you need.  The bed was comfortable, and it has adjustable air-conditioning and a dehumidifier, which is preferable to other hotels that keep the air-conditioning locked at say 24-25 degrees that may be too hot for some.   My request for a shaving kit was promptly answered and received within a few minutes.  Overall, the service was very good. 

My one suggestion: the hotel should buy a couple of irons, so guests can borrow if they need to iron their clothes.  You don't necessarily need one in each room but being able to borrow one when needed is very convenient.  

Otherwise, I think this hotel offers very good value for the price.

2. The facilities and environment are quite comfortable, pure Japanese style, and it has been carefully built. There are also many public spaces, which are much larger than the public areas of general downtown hotels, which is a plus.
3. The quality of the room is OK, there are not many furnitures, no sofas, the level is not up to five stars, but it is above four stars. The full open design is very comfortable for one person to live in, and the supplies are very good, exceeding four stars.
4. The guys at the front desk are very good. They feel like i people, introverted, but they will answer all questions and respond to all requests. They just didn't tell me that there was a cake in the refrigerator in the room when I checked in, which made me think it was left by the previous customer. It was the cleaning lady who told me that I could eat it. It's bright and leisurely, not bad. I hope the guys can take the initiative to introduce various hotel service details.
5. There are many small details. There are personal care products for self-collection at the elevator entrance, and there is a small box that actually has hairpins and sanitary napkins for girls, which is very loving! There are many snacks in the room, and the drinks in the refrigerator are also quite special. I don‚Äôt know if they can be eaten, but they seem to be free, which is very considerate;

7 They also gave me a forest fragrance essential oil from the hotel. I like it very much and will always remember this hotel;
8 Disadvantages: The room windows are not soundproof at all, which is a bit troublesome for light sleepers. The noise from the street is very clear at night. The room is equipped with earplugs, which is somewhat useful. Or you can use the Bluetooth speaker in the room to play some music

Because there were photos of meditation and gong bathing sound bowls in the store, I thought this was a hotel with a "realm". I didn't experience the package package because I was very dissatisfied with the hotel.
Unsatisfactory service:
1. Checked in on the 26th. That night, the guy at the front desk had a very bad attitude. He was lazy and tired. He didn't feel like "checking in" at all, even though he so-called upgraded the room for me (I blindly guessed it was because I brought my room). small children), for me personally, there is no sense of upgrade. They all cater more for group meals and we are the individual travelers. They didn't tell me that I could make a reservation or what I could eat. Almost the best thing I have seen in other hotels is the front desk. The service will make you feel really relaxed after a long day of fatigue. I wanted to change hotels from then on, but I resisted, thinking maybe the room would be nice.

2. The hotel does not deliver takeaways, and all takeaways are placed in the lobby. If you are a very "realm" hotel with good service and good facilities, I can also go up and down, but because the service facilities are not good, this will only Lower your favorability and make you even more dissatisfied.
The hotel can ask security to deliver its own meals, but there are no robots or staff to deliver takeaways, and their front desk is almost lazy or tired. Then please let us "individual travelers" who are not allowed to reserve meals, can only order takeout or run away by ourselves.

Dissatisfaction with facilities:
The hotel focuses on Japanese style and will be opened in 2020. It is smart. I thought it would suit young people,
1. First of all, the air conditioner cannot be adjusted. It is a central air conditioner. That is to say, if you are afraid of cold or heat, you cannot adjust it according to your temperature. In 2023, there will still be hotels that cannot adjust the temperature. I thought the one I was staying in was What a third-tier suburban hotel.
2. Hair dryer, I probably have the heavy, hot and loud one used in reception rooms when I was in college.
3. There are very few bedside plugs, and none of them are empty. If you want to plug in a charger, you need to remove the phone plug or purifier or stereo.

Dissatisfaction with the environment:
It was very noisy outside the room, next to the street, and the sound of trash being taken out in the morning and evening was very noisy. I don't blame the hotel for this.
However, the room (our two rooms) toilets and sewers all smelled bad. Even though the cleaning lady took care of it one day, there was still a smell in the shower the next day.

I saw a very profound negative review. He said that the hotel spent all the renovation costs on the first floor.
Indeed, I will not come again anyway, and this experience will be added to my public account article. I will not experience it again, and it will protect people around me from lightning.

I originally longed for Yinbo, after all, I liked it very much, but in the end, this hotel was not only disappointing, but also disappointing.
If this hotel is just opened with the idea of ‚Äã‚Äãcalming down city dwellers, it would be better to reflect on the idea.
